		NOT = { has_idea = md_closed_economy }

				remove_idea = consumption_economy
				add_idea = export_economy
			}
		}

			limit = { has_idea = mixed_economy }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = mixed_economy
				add_idea = export_economy
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_political_power = 50
		}
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: focus ALG_export_driven_growth executed"
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		base = 1
	}
